--
-- Table structure for table `EMP_MONTHLY_SALARY`
--

) ENGINE=MyISAM  DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 AUTO_INCREMENT=4414 ;

--
-- Table structure for table `jppl_monthly_salary_variables`
--

CREATE TABLE `jppl_monthly_salary_variables` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `emp_id` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `ot` float DEFAULT NULL,
  `spl_allowance` float DEFAULT NULL,
  `absent_days` float DEFAULT NULL,
  `loan_amount` float DEFAULT NULL,
  `cuppon_amount` float DEFAULT NULL,
  `other_deduction` float DEFAULT NULL,
  `mode_date` datetime NOT NULL,
  `salary_month` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `salary_year` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `user_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `last_update` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM  DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 AUTO_INCREMENT=1219 ;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `jppl_price_master`
--

CREATE TABLE `jppl_price_master` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `product_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `unit_price` float NOT NULL,
  `status` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `last_update` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=1 ;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `jppl_print_master`
--

CREATE TABLE `jppl_print_master` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `publication` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `date` date NOT NULL,
  `print_order` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `color_page` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `bw_page` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `user_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `location` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `last_update` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `jppl_product_master`
--

CREATE TABLE `jppl_product_master` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `name` varchar(80) NOT NULL,
  `type` varchar(80) NOT NULL,
  `unit` enum('Kg','ltr','Nos') NOT NULL DEFAULT 'Kg',
  `status` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `last_update` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=1 ;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `jppl_stock_ledger`
--

CREATE TABLE `jppl_stock_ledger` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `product_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `location` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `transaction_date` date NOT NULL,
  `transaction_reference_no` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `unit_quantity` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `box_quantity` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `transaction_type` enum('Purchase','Sale','Transfer-in','Transfer-out','Transfer-pending','Stock_correction','Consumption') NOT NULL,
  `remarks` varchar(80) NOT NULL,
  `user_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `last_update` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  UNIQUE KEY `id` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=1 ;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `jppl_stock_master`
--

CREATE TABLE `jppl_stock_master` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `product_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `location` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `ledger_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `unit_available` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `box_available` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `last_transaction` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `last_update` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=1 ;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `jppl_transaction_master`
--

CREATE TABLE `jppl_transaction_master` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `dept_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `transaction_head` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `location` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `amount` float NOT NULL,
  `payment_date` date NOT NULL,
  `payment_mode` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `instrument_number` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `instrument_date` date NOT NULL,
  `payment_type` enum('Debit','Credit') NOT NULL,
  `user_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `last_update` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=1 ;

--
-- Table structure for table `jppl_user_master`
--

CREATE TABLE `jppl_user_master` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `profile_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `name` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `email` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `mobile` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `user_type` enum('admin','account','dispatch','hr') NOT NULL,
  `password` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `status` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `last_update` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `email` (`email`),
  UNIQUE KEY `mobile` (`mobile`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;
